## MathFractionFactory class

 Allows to create a math fraction
 
 For COM comparibility
 
### MathFractionFactory {#MathFractionFactory}

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| MathFractionFactory() |  |

 **Returns:**
MathFractionFactory


---


### createMathFraction {#createMathFraction}

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| createMathFraction ([MathBlock](../mathblock), [MathBlock](../mathblock), int) | Creates a math fraction |

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |

[MathFraction](../mathfraction)
